  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_54298273-0e30-4fbb-83e1-7e6e5a6b541a'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer17048069587934651083">Practicing law in a large partnership, Sydney Jones was primed for making partner. Then her life turned upside down after a disagreement with her boss at Birdman & Birdman.<br/><br/>Leaving the office, she was swiftly kidnapped and taken to her assailants’ hideaway, beaten, and raped.   <span id="freeText17048069587934651083" style="display:none">Practicing law in a large partnership, Sydney Jones was primed for making partner. Then her life turned upside down after a disagreement with her boss at Birdman &amp; Birdman.<br /><br />Leaving the office, she was swiftly kidnapped and taken to her assailants’ hideaway, beaten, and raped. With no memory of whom she was put her at a disadvantage with her captors. Through gritted teeth, she promised a day of repercussions for their actions while mentally visualizing her revenge.<br /><br />Warned by her assailants to keep her mouth shut or else, she was delivered to her home. Not recognizing her former living quarters, she was careful in exploring her options for regaining her memory.<br /><br />Piecing together the reasons for her kidnapping brought her into contact with people, some she could trust and others risky. The problem was the amnesia prevented her from recognizing the difference.<br /><br />Tapped for crime once nudged her toward caution for something afoul was going on at Birdman &amp; Birdman. She prepared for a fight. With a vision of fury she made a chilling decision – never to be a victim again.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17048069587934651083" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer5586202019215127161">I read this twice. It had a very interesting lead in. The middle part was a bit of who was doing what and where. The ending wasn't quite what I was anticipated. I thought maybe the lead character needed a little more of a highlighting role. I felt it was a good read. </span>

<div id="review_3551847513" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3551847513" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3551847513?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781733685801" href="/book/show/51928234-primed-for-revenge">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3551847513" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10039618567379996132">‘It wasn’t like Sydney Jones to just up and disappear…’<br/><br/>Author Carolyn M. Bowen has a background in life planning and career development with advanced studies in psychology, adult learning, and career development, Her initial publication was CROSS-TIES (an historical romance), followed by THE LONG ROAD HOME (romance mystery) and CROSS-STEPPING YOUR WAY TO SUCCESS (life coaching short book), and now she concentrates her scriptive gifts on writing mysteries. She has created a strong female protagon</span>
  <span id="freeText10039618567379996132" style="display:none">‘It wasn’t like Sydney Jones to just up and disappear…’<br /><br />Author Carolyn M. Bowen has a background in life planning and career development with advanced studies in psychology, adult learning, and career development, Her initial publication was CROSS-TIES (an historical romance), followed by THE LONG ROAD HOME (romance mystery) and CROSS-STEPPING YOUR WAY TO SUCCESS (life coaching short book), and now she concentrates her scriptive gifts on writing mysteries. She has created a strong female protagonist in Sydney Jones, a lawyer, and PRIMED FOR REVENGE is Book 1 of her Sydney Jones Series of novels. <br /><br />Using her depth of experience in examining people’s behavior in addition to her keen sense of place (likely due to her extensive travels to other cultures), Carolyn presents in this book a well sculpted central character in Sydney Jones, and from the impetus of this initial book, the series merits our full attention. <br /><br />The incident that is the core of this thriller is discovered in the opening paragraphs – ‘‘She awakened not knowing where she was or how she got there…She’d kill to remember her past and what brought her to this place and time, but she figured she wasn’t a killer, as she was the one beaten beyond recognition. She felt a lump growing on the side of her head peeking out from the blood-smeared follicles, The stench of blood was something she could never grow accustomed to…She had no idea how long she’d been there and when, if ever, anyone would return, especially her accosters…’<br /><br />How this kidnapping plays such a key role in the story is explained in the synopsis; ‘Practicing law in a large partnership, Sydney Jones was primed for making partner. Then her life turned upside down after a disagreement with her boss at Birdman &amp; Birdman. Leaving the office, she was swiftly kidnapped and taken to her assailants’ hideaway, beaten, and raped. With no memory of whom she was put her at a disadvantage with her captors. Through gritted teeth, she promised a day of repercussions for their actions while mentally visualizing her revenge. Warned by her assailants to keep her mouth shut or else, she was delivered to her home. Not recognizing her former living quarters, she was careful in exploring her options for regaining her memory. Piecing together the reasons for her kidnapping brought her into contact with people, some she could trust and others risky. The problem was the amnesia prevented her from recognizing the difference. Tapped for crime once nudged her toward caution for something afoul was going on at Birdman &amp; Birdman. She prepared for a fight. With a vision of fury she made a chilling decision – never to be a victim again.’<br /><br />This is a ‘hold your breath’ quality mystery, well written and well paced, an adventure that introduces a fine series. Highly recommended.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10039618567379996132" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2871663688" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2871663688" />
    <a title="Jewel Hart" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56470711-jewel-hart"><img alt="Jewel Hart" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595707974p2/56470711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2871663688?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jewel Hart" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jewel Hart" href="/user/show/56470711-jewel-hart">Jewel Hart</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781733685801" href="/book/show/51928234-primed-for-revenge">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2871663688" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10675153248859153696">Primed For Revenge, the first book in a new and exciting psychological thriller series by Carolyn M. Bowen, brings readers a captivating mystery filled with crime, conspiracy and deceit. The author pulls no punches with a dynamic observation into the emotions and actions taken when one’s life is confronted with unexpected, debilitating and life changing events, of the horrific kind.<br/><br/>Sydney Jones has a bright career as an attorney at a large law firm, prepared to become a partner. However, a disag</span>
  <span id="freeText10675153248859153696" style="display:none">Primed For Revenge, the first book in a new and exciting psychological thriller series by Carolyn M. Bowen, brings readers a captivating mystery filled with crime, conspiracy and deceit. The author pulls no punches with a dynamic observation into the emotions and actions taken when one’s life is confronted with unexpected, debilitating and life changing events, of the horrific kind.<br /><br />Sydney Jones has a bright career as an attorney at a large law firm, prepared to become a partner. However, a disagreement with her boss at Birdman and Birdman, infuriates Sydney and she does not take it lying down, causing unforeseen negative consequences.<br /><br />When she is kidnapped, tortured, brutally raped and returned to her home, Sydney is warned to keep her mouth shut. Sydney has no idea why she was targeted and she has now lost her memory too. Now, suffering from amnesia, she tries to get her life back. She begins to exercise and work out and goes to the gun range, learns to handle and shoot a gun. She becomes stronger, learns to protect herself and tries to overcome such a horrific attack on her body and life. She wants revenge and gets prepared for a fight. As she starts to regain some of her memory and put the pieces together, disturbing events are brewing behind the scenes while deceptive friendships and situations come her way.<br /><br />Primed For Revenge by Carolyn Bowen is an exceptional crime and mystery story filled with intrigue, romance, action and unexpected surprises that kept me on the edge of my seat from start to finish, which ended with a tremendous twist. The exciting, deep, complex and fully believable plot is brought to life with Bowen’s expressive descriptive words, vivid scenery, settings, and of course, the shocking scenes. Sydney Jones is a fabulous character with strength and determination. She should not trust those who come to befriend and help her, but takes her chances. Because after all, she did forget everyone she knew, and even the house she lived in. What a struggle for one woman to endure. Many readers will identify with her vulnerability, and be inspired and encouraged by the strong woman she becomes after being victimized in such a brutal manner.<br /><br />Carolyn M. Bowen has captured the essence of various authentic, interesting and compelling characters. She has an original clever ability for writing about fascinating people, unique places and astonishing unusual occurrences. The dialog between the characters is brilliant and impressive, sometimes heated and many times, warm.<br /><br />Overall, Primed For Revenge by Carolyn M. Bowen is an entertaining read, with a great fulfilling plot and storyline that flows nicely, is easy to follow and become engrossed in. The characters all play an important and vital part to this creative and original novel which is the beginning of a remarkable new psychological thrillers series, entitled Sydney Jones Novel Series by Carolyn M. Bowen. Don’t miss out on this captivating, compelling and thrilling 5 star read!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10675153248859153696" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText12808831209628100390" style="display:none">In Primed for Revenge, Sydney Jones, a lawyer working in a large law firm, becomes the target of a brutal kidnapping and rape that leaves her suffering from amnesia. As she slowly regains her memories and tries to build her life, deceit comes disguised in the form of friendship. For gullible Sydney, who has always lived a sheltered life, it is about time she learns to protect what’s her own.<br /><br />Bowen paints a compelling picture of good, everyday people becoming victims of financial frauds; the consistent gullibility and lack of caution on Sydney’s part create an imagery that will resonate with many readers. The plot is a bit muddled, but characters are interesting while Bowen explores a larger question: how far should a woman go to protect her dignity? <br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3459938717?book_show_action=true">Jul 24, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carolyn Bowen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carolyn Bowen" href="/user/show/31968007-carolyn-bowen">Carolyn Bowen</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3459938717" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2728935033335764957">5 Stars for Primed for Revenge by Carolyn Bowen<br/>Reviewed by Ruffina Oserio for Readers’ Favorite<br/><br/>Primed For Revenge: Sydney Jones Novel Series by Carolyn M Bowen is a spellbinding psychological thriller with a rock-solid female protagonist: Sydney Jones works for Birdman & Birdman and at the time she is looking for bigger engagements in the firm, there is fallout with her boss. As if this wasn’t enough to rattle her nerves, she is abducted as she leaves the office. She is badly beaten and raped an</span>
  <span id="freeText2728935033335764957" style="display:none">5 Stars for Primed for Revenge by Carolyn Bowen<br />Reviewed by Ruffina Oserio for Readers’ Favorite<br /><br />Primed For Revenge: Sydney Jones Novel Series by Carolyn M Bowen is a spellbinding psychological thriller with a rock-solid female protagonist: Sydney Jones works for Birdman &amp; Birdman and at the time she is looking for bigger engagements in the firm, there is fallout with her boss. As if this wasn’t enough to rattle her nerves, she is abducted as she leaves the office. She is badly beaten and raped and sent home with warnings to never talk about the kidnapping. What is worse is that she has lost a great deal of her memory, but she hasn’t forgotten her resolve for revenge. <br /><br />This is an interesting story about a character who is deeply hurt and damaged and who must navigate a very dangerous landscape to determine who kidnapped and hurt her and why. Her biggest challenge is identifying the right people to talk to. The reader follows her, feeling her pain and seeing her struggle with her options. Primed For Revenge is a sophisticated, deftly written thriller with a protagonist that instantly captured my attention. The pathos is strong as the reader watches her go through the rough experience. Her inner transformation and the quest for revenge are so real, reflecting the abuse she has experienced. <br /><br />The writing is wonderful, and Carolyn M Bowen comes across as a perfect wordsmith. Primed for Revenge: Sydney Jones Novel Series is very engaging, emotionally rich, and fast-paced. The kind of book you read in one sitting. A highly recommended read – 5 Stars<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_2871662567" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2871662567" />
    <a title="Jewel Hart" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56470711-jewel-hart"><img alt="Jewel Hart" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595707974p2/56470711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2871662567?book_show_action=true">Jun 25, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jewel Hart" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jewel Hart" href="/user/show/56470711-jewel-hart">Jewel Hart</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2871662567" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10817264926756280930">Primed For Revenge, the first book in a new and exciting psychological thriller series by Carolyn M. Bowen, brings readers a captivating mystery filled with crime, conspiracy and deceit. The author pulls no punches with a dynamic observation into the emotions and actions taken when one’s life is confronted with unexpected, debilitating and life changing events, of the horrific kind.<br/><br/>Sydney Jones has a bright career as an attorney at a large law firm, prepared to become a partner. However, a disag</span>
  <span id="freeText10817264926756280930" style="display:none">Primed For Revenge, the first book in a new and exciting psychological thriller series by Carolyn M. Bowen, brings readers a captivating mystery filled with crime, conspiracy and deceit. The author pulls no punches with a dynamic observation into the emotions and actions taken when one’s life is confronted with unexpected, debilitating and life changing events, of the horrific kind.<br /><br />Sydney Jones has a bright career as an attorney at a large law firm, prepared to become a partner. However, a disagreement with her boss at Birdman and Birdman, infuriates Sydney and she does not take it lying down, causing unforeseen negative consequences.<br /><br />When she is kidnapped, tortured, brutally raped and returned to her home, Sydney is warned to keep her mouth shut. Sydney has no idea why she was targeted and she has now lost her memory too. Now, suffering from amnesia, she tries to get her life back. She begins to exercise and work out and goes to the gun range, learns to handle and shoot a gun. She becomes stronger, learns to protect herself and tries to overcome such a horrific attack on her body and life. She wants revenge and gets prepared for a fight. As she starts to regain some of her memory and put the pieces together, disturbing events are brewing behind the scenes while deceptive friendships and situations come her way.<br /><br />Primed For Revenge by Carolyn Bowen is an exceptional crime and mystery story filled with intrigue, romance, action and unexpected surprises that kept me on the edge of my seat from start to finish, which ended with a tremendous twist. The exciting, deep, complex and fully believable plot is brought to life with Bowen’s expressive descriptive words, vivid scenery, settings, and of course, the shocking scenes. Sydney Jones is a fabulous character with strength and determination. She should not trust those who come to befriend and help her, but takes her chances. Because after all, she did forget everyone she knew, and even the house she lived in. What a struggle for one woman to endure. Many readers will identify with her vulnerability, and be inspired and encouraged by the strong woman she becomes after being victimized in such a brutal manner.<br /><br />Carolyn M. Bowen has captured the essence of various authentic, interesting and compelling characters. She has an original clever ability for writing about fascinating people, unique places and astonishing unusual occurrences. The dialog between the characters is brilliant and impressive, sometimes heated and many times, warm.<br /><br />Overall, Primed For Revenge by Carolyn M. Bowen is an entertaining read, with a great fulfilling plot and storyline that flows nicely, is easy to follow and become engrossed in. The characters all play an important and vital part to this creative and original novel which is the beginning of a remarkable new psychological thrillers series, entitled Sydney Jones Novel Series by Carolyn M. Bowen. Don’t miss out on this captivating, compelling and thrilling 5 star read!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10817264926756280930" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2708963069" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2708963069" />
    <a title="Kate" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48870407-kate"><img alt="Kate" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466689015p2/48870407.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2708963069?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kate" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kate" href="/user/show/48870407-kate">Kate</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781733685801" href="/book/show/51928234-primed-for-revenge">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2708963069" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer467710423421556684">Primed for Revenge by Carolyn M. Bowen has a kidnapping, rape, embezzlement, murder, deception, and even romance. Sydney Jones is a lawyer in a large firm. She is kidnapped, raped, drugged and finally released and she has no memory of who she is or of being kidnapped. The events that bring her memory back and the people who helped her make for a suspense filled story. Sydney is able to deal with many problems and maybe she will even find romance and love along the way. <br/><br/>I received this book as a </span>
  <span id="freeText467710423421556684" style="display:none">Primed for Revenge by Carolyn M. Bowen has a kidnapping, rape, embezzlement, murder, deception, and even romance. Sydney Jones is a lawyer in a large firm. She is kidnapped, raped, drugged and finally released and she has no memory of who she is or of being kidnapped. The events that bring her memory back and the people who helped her make for a suspense filled story. Sydney is able to deal with many problems and maybe she will even find romance and love along the way. <br /><br />I received this book as a gift and I always review every book that I read. I found the plot and characters to be well developed. There are no cliff hangers in this book, but there is potential for additional follow-on stories. If you enjoy legal procedures, court trials and suspense, this book is for you. Enjoy.</span>
  <a data-text-id="467710423421556684" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText7107514714619520629" style="display:none">A random find on Netgalley for this one. It seemed like we would get a good story and a kickass heroine. <br /><br /><br /><br />The story follows Syndey who was kidnapped leaving her office. Beaten and raped to the point of having memory loss. Slowly piecing together her memory and the reason why she was attacked she is ready for a fight and to never be a victim again. <br /><br /><br /><br />This had all the makings to be a great story filled with crime and drama and a kickass heroine. It was intriguing for sure. I enjoyed the mystery and the slow-build-up and uncovering of information. But the narrative was sooooooooo slow. <br /><br /><br /><br />I liked Syndey and I felt sooooo bad for her. She had SO many bad things happen to her even outside of the beating and rape. Poor girl. I can see her snapping a bit there. Any normal person would.<br /><br /><br /><br />Super bummed by her one friend (no spoilers) but I was so upset. <br /><br /><br /><br />That Walker was interesting. Didn't trust Walker....but it was so hard to trust anyone in this novel. <br /><br /><br /><br />I did enjoy the story overall even though the narrative was SO slow and I felt like nothing was going to happen. I wanted Sydney to go off the rails right away! <br /><br /><br /><br />Overall, pretty interesting and I was intrigued in the story and the characters even though it dragged on and on. It took forever, but when things did happen I was hooked. I'll give this 3 stars. </span>

She is kidnapped, raped and beaten and has no idea why. When she is finally dumped back at her home, she has no idea who she is or if this is her home as she is suffering from amnesia. Judith, from her law firm, has been trying to find Sydney and hires a private investigator. At first, Sydney rebuffs Judith, but then realizes that she needs someone who knows who she is and allows her in t</span>
  <span id="freeText9286713803638750473" style="display:none">Sydney Jones has made a success of her law career, but when she disagrees with her boss her life is upended. She is kidnapped, raped and beaten and has no idea why. When she is finally dumped back at her home, she has no idea who she is or if this is her home as she is suffering from amnesia. Judith, from her law firm, has been trying to find Sydney and hires a private investigator. At first, Sydney rebuffs Judith, but then realizes that she needs someone who knows who she is and allows her in to her home and life. Installing a gym in her home and practicing at the gun range, Sydney is now stronger and can protect herself as her memories begin to resurface. In my opinion, the whole plot was questionable in that she would go through what she did and not contact the police, especially since she was suffering from amnesia. Why did she trust Judith? Why did she trust the private investigator? For a smart lawyer and supposedly out for revenge, she seems to accept what she is told by people that she does not know or remember. I had too many questions as the story and the characters seemed impossible for me to believe. I received an advance review copy at no cost and without obligation for an honest review. (by paytonpuppy)</span>

When Sydney was leaving the office, she was kidnapped, beaten and raped. <br/><br/>One thing Sydney learned that day was that as a woman, she is the weaker sex.   <span id="freeText15372003783079910615" style="display:none">Primed For Revenge by the author Carolyn M Bowen is the first book in the Sydney Jones Series. It is a crime fiction. Protagonist of the story is Sydney Jones. She is an employee of Birdman &amp; Birdman. She went into an argument with her boss. When Sydney was leaving the office, she was kidnapped, beaten and raped. <br /><br />One thing Sydney learned that day was that as a woman, she is the weaker sex. She was sent home but she wasn't allowed to reveal any details about her kidnapping to anyone. Even though Sydney don't remember how and when she got kidnapped, she was determined to find it and take revenge. <br /><br />The plot of the story is very intriguing. If you love reading mystery thrillers, then you can't afford to miss to read this one.</span>

BOWEN is a mystery author who has gained lot of fame with her writing and her Sydney Jones series is a hit.<br /><br />💌I am the kind of person who is always up for this kind of crime and mystery novel and after reading this first part of this series, I can't wait to read the next part😍</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('lpBx1rW79UPXdmNk2GkMZiNhBAeXSJJ5tZgN5KbZdtuaadPBWs0QFk5liiQafO3n39MLuzUxAW6gUGg9ISSsIQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('peIp4PFobTT2D8vnvFMh+byZwY05qWjbMkjJB1nOhS6pG4v3Hh6IYW8cIqd+RsB4QCvOMZvQ+8wngKze3jNf1A==')})
  }
